<h6 class="kt-adv-heading9_725cec-e0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading9_725cec-e0">so glad you&#8217;re here</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading9_64688d-57 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading9_64688d-57">Hi! We&#8217;re Melissa and Austin&#8230;</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">With&nbsp;<em>four kids in tow</em>&nbsp;we’ve navigated the highs and lows of family travel through every stage of parenthood.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">From sleepless nights with newborns to the boundless energy of toddlers, and now navigating the unique beauty of traveling with older kids and teens, we’ve experienced it all and can’t wait to share our tips with you!<br><br>As chronic researchers, <strong>we sift through the mountains of information to uncover the absolute best adventures</strong>, crafting them into perfect, kid-friendly itineraries that are tried, tested and loved by our family.</p>
